	<script type="text/javaScript" language="javascript">	
	
	var firstTime = new Date();
	var first_dt = firstTime.getFullYear() + "-" + ((firstTime.getMonth()+1)<10?'0':'') +(firstTime.getMonth()+1) + "-" + (firstTime.getDate()<10?'0':'') +firstTime.getDate() + "-" + (firstTime.getHours()<10?'0':'') +firstTime.getHours() + "-" + (firstTime.getMinutes()<10?'0':'') +firstTime.getMinutes() + "-" + (firstTime.getSeconds()<10?'0':'') +firstTime.getSeconds();
	first_dt = first_dt.replace(/-/gi,"");
	
		$(document).ready(function(){	 
			//1분후에 새로고침 버튼 활성화 
			//$("#reflesh").attr("disabled",true);
			//setTimeout(fnViewButton, 60000); 
			
			//alert("연휴 추첨발표 관계로 16시까지\n\n전지역 객실현황 메뉴를 제한합니다.");
			//location.href='/reservation.online.roomUseCalSts.dp/dmparse.dm';
			//return;
			
		}); 
		
		function fnViewButton(){
			$("#reflesh").attr("disabled",false);
		}
				
		function fnMove(move){
			if('5551000' == move){
				$(location).attr('href','/reservation.online.roomUseCalSts.dp/dmparse.dm'); 
			}else if('5551001' == move){
				if('Y' == 'Y') {
					param = '?nonSearchYN=Y';
				} else {
					param = '';
				}
				
				$(location).attr('href','/reservation.online.roomUseTotCalSts.dp/dmparse.dm'+param);  
			}
		}
		
		function fnSchRsv(status) {	

			var nowTime = new Date();
			var now_dt = nowTime.getFullYear() + "-" + ((nowTime.getMonth()+1)<10?'0':'') +(nowTime.getMonth()+1) + "-" + (nowTime.getDate()<10?'0':'') +nowTime.getDate() + "-" + (nowTime.getHours()<10?'0':'') +nowTime.getHours() + "-" + (nowTime.getMinutes()<10?'0':'') +nowTime.getMinutes() + "-" + (nowTime.getSeconds()<10?'0':'') +nowTime.getSeconds();
			now_dt = now_dt.replace(/-/gi,"");
			var d = now_dt - first_dt;
			if(status == 'toDay'){
				if(d < 10){
					alert("새로고침은 "+ (10-d) +"초 후에 가능합니다.");
					return;
				}
			}
			
			var intDiffDate = diffDate('20220118', $("#checkInDate").val());			
			
			if(intDiffDate > 0 || status == 'Next' || status == 'toDay') {
				$("#selectStatus").val(status);				
				url = "/reservation.online.roomUseTotCalSts.dp/dmparse.dm";
				loadFrm("잠시만 기다려주세요...", "resvInfoListVo", "post", url);				
				return false;
			} else {
				alert("오늘 이후로만 조회 가능합니다.");
				return false;
			}			
		}
		 
		 
		function fnResvOk(useDate, condoCode, dongCode, pyungCode, roomKindCode, rsvGubun) {
			var strUseDate = useDate.replace(/-/g, '');
			
			$("#checkInDate").val(strUseDate);
			$("#condoCode").val(condoCode);
			$("#dongCode").val(dongCode);
			$("#pyungCode").val(pyungCode);
			$("#pyungType").val(roomKindCode);	
			$("#roomKindCode").val(roomKindCode);
											
			if(rsvGubun == 'R') {
				$("#resvInfoListVo").attr({method:"post", action:"/reservation.online.roomUForm.dp/dmparse.dm"}).submit();
			} else if(rsvGubun == 'W') {
				$("#resvInfoListVo").attr({method:"post", action:"/reservation.online.resvRoomWaitForm.dp/dmparse.dm"}).submit();	
			}
		}
				
		
		function fnExcel() {		
			$("#resvInfoListVo").attr({method:"post", action:"/reservation.online.roomUseTotCalStExcel.dp/dmparse.dm"}).submit();
			return false;
		}
	</script>

<script>

var saupjangCodeGlobal = '';
saupjangCode = '';


$(window).load(function(){
	if(saupjangCode == "05" || saupjangCode == "22" ||  saupjangCode == "507" ||  saupjangCode == "508" ){
			$("#quick").animate({"top":90-$(window).scrollTop()},500);
	}

	//사업장일 경우, 오션베이, 마리나베이 코드 추가 팝업레이어 line-height값 조정
	if (saupjangCode == '19' || saupjangCode == "20" || saupjangCode == "21" || saupjangCode == "30" || saupjangCode == "32" || saupjangCode == "29" || saupjangCode == "58" || saupjangCode == "57") {
		$(".popupLayer_sf").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_sol").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_calm").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_belle").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_moon").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_hue").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_oplay").css("line-height","13px");
		$(".popupLayer_oadventure").css("line-height","13px");
	}		
	//사업장 코드 별로 대메뉴 컬러 변경
	if (saupjangCode == "19") {			//양평
		$("#gnb li a").hover(function() {
			$(this).css("color", "#3677bc");
		}, function(){
			$(this).css("color", "#333333");
		});
	} else if (saupjangCode == "20") {	//경주
		$("#gnb li a").hover(function() {
			$(this).css("color", "#865e3d");
		}, function(){
			$(this).css("color", "#333333");
		});
	} else if (saupjangCode == "21") {	//단양
		$("#gnb li a").hover(function() {
			$(this).css("color", "#226738");
		}, function(){
			$(this).css("color", "#333333");
		});
	} else if (saupjangCode == "30") {	//변산
		$("#gnb li a").hover(function() {
			$(this).css("color", "#691011");
		}, function(){
			$(this).css("color", "#333333");
		});
	} else if (saupjangCode == "32") {	//거제
		$("#gnb li a").hover(function() {
			$(this).css("color", "#6e97ec");
		}, function(){
			$(this).css("color", "#333333");
		});
	} else if (saupjangCode == "29") {	//제주
		$("#gnb li a").hover(function() {
			$(this).css("color", "#44afb2");
		}, function(){
			$(this).css("color", "#333333");
		});
	}		
});

function globalActive(){

	if(identity == 1){
		$("#global .active .container").hide();
		$("#global .active .reisure").show();
	}else{
		$("#global .active .container").hide();
		$("#global .active .resortb").show();
	}
	

	$("#global .active").slideDown(500);
	$("header").animate({"top":95},500);
	//$("nav").animate({"top":195},500);
	global = true;
	active = true;
}

function quickMenuDown(){
	$("#eventZone").animate({"top":90-$(window).scrollTop()},500);
	$("#smartMenu").animate({"top":90-$(window).scrollTop()},500);
}
//동적폼 생성해서 인트로 페이지로 보냄
function move_page(val) {
	var $form = $('<form></form>');
	$form.hide();
	$form.attr('action', '/');
	$form.attr('method', 'get');	//페이지 이동(뒤로가기) 문제로 GET으로 변경
	$form.append("<input type='hidden' name='pageNum' value='"+ val +"' /> ");
	$form.appendTo('body');
	$form.submit();
}

//마우스 이벤트 체크
$("html, body").on('mousewheel DOMMouseScroll', function(e) {
	if ($(".popupLayer_sf").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_sol").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_calm").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_belle").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_moon").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_hue").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_oplay").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_oadventure").is(":visible")) {
		$(".popupLayer_sf").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_sol").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_calm").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_belle").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_moon").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_hue").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_oplay").css("display","none");
		$(".popupLayer_oadventure").css("display","none");
	}
});
//다른 GNB대메뉴 선택시 숨김 처리
$(document).ready(function() {
	$('html').on('click', function(e) { 
		if(!$(e.target).is(".select_sf, .select_sol, .select_calm, .select_belle, .select_moon, .select_hue, .select_oplay, .select_oadventure")) { 
			if ($(".popupLayer_sf").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_sol").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_calm").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_belle").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_moon").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_hue").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_oplay").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_oadventure").is(":visible")) {
				$(".popupLayer_sf").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_sol").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_calm").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_belle").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_moon").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_hue").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_oplay").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_oadventure").css("display","none");
			}
		} 
	});
});

	$(document).ready(function() {
		//소노펠리체 시작
		//$('.select_sf').mouseover(function() {
		$('.select_sf').click(function() {
			if ($(".popupLayer_sol").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_calm").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_belle").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_moon").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_hue").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_oplay").is(":visible") || $(".popupLayer_oadventure").is(":visible")) {

				$(".popupLayer_belle").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_moon").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_hue").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_oplay").css("display","none");
				$(".popupLayer_oadventure").css("display","none");
			} 
			var popH = $(this).offset().top;
			var popW = $(this).offset().left;
			 			 
			//var divLeft = popW + 90;
			//var divTop = popH;
			var divLeft = popW - 1;
			var divTop = popH + 37;

			$('.popupLayer_sf').css({
				"top": divTop,
				"left": divLeft,
				"position": "fixed",
				"font-size": "13px",
				"width": "200px"
			});//.show();
			
			$(".popupLayer_sf").toggle('fade',100);
		});
		
		$(".sf_area").hover(function() {
			var idx = $(".sf_area").index(this);
			$(".sf_area:eq("+idx+")").addClass("sf_area_over");
			}, function () {
				var idx = $(".sf_area").index(this);
				$(".sf_area:eq("+idx+")").removeClass("sf_area_over");
			}
		);
		
		$(".popupLayer_sf").mouseleave(function() {
			$(this).css("display","none");
		});

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
	//다국어선택
	$('.lang > a').on('click', function(){
		$(this).next().toggle();
		$(this).toggleClass('on');
	});

	$('.lang_type').on('mouseleave', function(){//2016-09-26 수정
		$('.lang > a').removeClass('on');
		$('.lang_type').hide();
	});
	
	
	
/* 	$("#dmSearchKey").keyup(function(e) {
		if(e.keyCode == 13) {
			dmGoSearch();
		}
	}); */	
	$("#dmSearchKey").live('keypress', function(e){
		if(e.keyCode == 13){
			var keyword = $("#dmSearchKey").val().trim();
			if(keyword == ""){
				alert('검색어를 입력하세요.');
				return false;
			}
			keyword = encodeURI(keyword);
			//$("#kwd").val(keyword);
			//loadFrm('로딩중입니다...', 'findFrm', 'get', 'search/');
			$(location).attr("href", "/search/?kwd="+keyword+"&category=TOTAL&pageSize=5&sort=r&preKwd=");
			return false;
		}
	});
	
});

function dmGoSearch(){
	var keyword = $("#dmSearchKey").val().trim();
	if(keyword == ""){
		alert('검색어를 입력하세요.');
		return false;
	}
	keyword = encodeURI(keyword);
	//$("#kwd").val(keyword);
	//loadFrm('로딩중입니다...', 'findFrm', 'get', 'search/');
	$(location).attr("href", "/search/?kwd="+keyword+"&category=TOTAL&pageSize=5&sort=r&preKwd=");
	return false;
}

$(document).ready(function() {
	//통합검색
	$('.search').on('click', function(){
		$('.search_layer').show();
	});
	$('.search_layer a').on('click', function(){
		$('.search_layer').hide();
	});
});
</script>

				};
			}).blur(function(){ 
				var i = $(this); 
				if(i.val() == '' || i.val() == i.attr('placeholder')){
				var idName = i.attr("id");
					document.getElementById(idName).style.cssText="color:#999";
					if(this.type=='password'){
						i.addClass('password');
						this.type='text';
					}; 
					i.addClass('placeholder').val(i.attr('placeholder'));
				};
			}).blur().parents('form').submit(function(){ 
				$(this).find('[placeholder]').each(function(){
					var i = $(this);
					if(i.val() == i.attr('placeholder')) i.val('');
				});
			});
		};
    };
});

function DialogView(msg){
	var failTxtChk = '';
	var failTxtChk = "";
	/* if (failTxtChk == '') {
		failTxtChk = 1;
	} */
	//넘겨 받는값 강제 셋팅해서 span 강제 등록
	//console.log("가공전 메시지 : " + msg);
	msg = msg.replace(/</gi,"&lt;").replace(/prompt/gi,"").replace(/onerror/gi,"");
	msg = msg.replace(/\n\n\n/gi,"</span>")
	msg = msg.replace(/\n\n/gi,"<span>")
	msg = msg.replace(/\n/gi,"<br/>")
	//console.log("가공후 메시지 : " + msg);
	var msgcontent = "";
	if(msg.indexOf('h1') > -1){
		msgcontent = msg;
	}else{
		var htmldata = new Array();
		htmldata.push("<h1>알림</h1>");
		htmldata.push("<div class='content'>");
		htmldata.push(""+msg);
		htmldata.push("</div>");
		htmldata.push("<div class='footer'>");
		htmldata.push("	<img src='/img/front/popup/logo.gif' width='138' height='29' alt='DAEMYUNG RESORT' />");
		htmldata.push("</div>");
		htmldata.push("<a href='#DM' class='btn_close'><img src='/img/front/popup/btn_close.gif' width='18' height='18' alt='닫기' id='dialogClose'/></a>");		
		msgcontent = htmldata.join("");
	}
	$("#_dialogView").html(msgcontent);
	
	
	$elCnt = $("#_dialogView span").text();
	var cntLength = parseInt($elCnt.length);	//넘어온 msg값중 replace후 span 존재 유무로 판단 span 있음 1(5회 이하), 없음 0(5회 이상)
	//console.log("elCnt 값 : " + $elCnt);
	//console.log("cntLength 값 : " + cntLength);
	//console.log("failTxtChk 값 : " + failTxtChk);
	var failMsg = '';
	if ($elCnt != '' && failTxtChk == '0' && parseInt($elCnt) <= 4) {
		$("#_dialogView").addClass("_dialogView_more");
		$("div .popup").css("border-top","0");
		//console.log("5회 미만으로 틀렸어요");
		$("#_dialogView").empty();
		//$("#_dialogView").append("<div style='width:400px;height:300px;'></div>");
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='loginFailPop'>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failTitle'>로그인 <span style='color:#ff8000;'>" + $elCnt + "</span> 회 실패</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failContent'>아이디 또는 비밀번호가 일치하지 않습니다.<br>5회 이상 입력 오류 시 정보보호를 위해 로그인이 제한됩니다.</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBar'></div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failPwdInfo'><span style='font-weight:bold;'>[비밀번호 재설정]</span><br>기명회원과 D멤버스회원은 본인확인 후 비밀번호 재설정이 가능합니다.<br><span style='color:red;font-weight:bold;'>(단, 무기명회원 불가)</span></div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBar'></div><br>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='closeFailPop'>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBtnPwdChg'>비밀번호 재설정</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBtnClose'>닫 기</div><br>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failPopFooter'><img src='/img/front/popup/logo.gif' width='138' height='29'></div>"
		failMsg = failMsg + "</div>";
		
		$("#_dialogView").html(failMsg);
		
		$("#dialogPop").show();
	} else if ($elCnt != '' && failTxtChk == '0' && parseInt($elCnt) >= 5) {
		$("#_dialogView").addClass("_dialogView_more");
		$("div .popup").css("border-top","0");
		//console.log("5회 이상으로 틀렸어요");
		$("#_dialogView").empty();
		//$("#_dialogView").append("<div style='width:400px;height:300px;'></div>");
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='loginFailPop'>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failTitle'>로그인 실패</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failContent'>아이디 또는 비밀번호 5회 이상 입력 오류로 정보보호 규정상 <br>30분간 로그인이 제한됩니다. 30분 후 다시 시도하여 주십시오.</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBar'></div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failPwdInfo'><span style='font-weight:bold;'>[비밀번호 재설정]</span><br>기명회원과 D멤버스회원은 본인확인 후 비밀번호 재설정이 가능합니다.<br><span style='color:red;font-weight:bold;'>(단, 무기명회원 불가)</span></div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBar'></div><br>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='closeFailPop'>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBtnPwdChg'>비밀번호 재설정</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failBtnClose'>닫 기</div><br>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "</div>";
		failMsg = failMsg + "<div class='failPopFooter'><img src='/img/front/popup/logo.gif' width='138' height='29'></div>"
		failMsg = failMsg + "</div>";
		
		$("#_dialogView").html(failMsg);
		$("#dialogPop").show();
	} else if ($elCnt != '' && failTxtChk == '' && parseInt($elCnt) < 6) {	//페이지 이동후 뒤로가기시 창 미노출 처리
		$("#dialogPop").hide();
	} else {	//기존 팝업창
		$("#dialogPop").show();
	}

	/* 	var maskHeight = $(document).height();  
	var maskWidth = $(window).width();
	
	var dialogTop =  (maskHeight/3) - ($('#dialog-box').height());  
	var dialogLeft = (maskWidth/2) - ($('#dialog-box').width()/2); 
	
	$('#dialog-overlay').css({height:maskHeight, width:maskWidth}).show();
	$('#dialog-box').css({top:dialogTop, left:dialogLeft}).show();
	
	$('#dialog-message').html(message); */
};
</script>

<script>
function chg_url() {
	var params = new Array(), keys = new Array(), values = new Array();	//배열 초기화
	if (location.search) {
		var chgUrl; 
		var parameter = location.search;
		var paramIndex = parameter.indexOf("?");
		parameter = parameter.substring(paramIndex+1);
		
		for (var i = 0 ; location.search.split("&")[i] ; i++ ) {
			params[i] = parameter.split("&")[i];
			keys[i] = params[i].split("=")[0];
			values[i] = params[i].split("=")[0];
			//console.log(params[i]);
			//console.log(keys[i] + "i값 : " + i);
			if (keys[i] == 'failTxtChk') {
				chgUrl = '';
			} else {
				if (i == 1) {
					chgUrl = chgUrl + params[i]; 
				} else {
					chgUrl = chgUrl + "&" + params[i];	
				}
			}
		}
		return chgUrl;
	}
}

$(document).ready(function(){
	$(".failBtnClose").on("click", function() {
		$("#dialogPop").hide();
		history.pushState(null, null, "dmparse.dm?" + chg_url());	//주소창 재설정
	});
	
	$(".failBtnPwdChg").on("click", function() {
		history.pushState(null, null, "dmparse.dm?" + chg_url());	//주소창 재설정
		location.href='/etc.find.pwLost.dp/dmparse.dm?menuCd=6640000&failYn=0';
	});
});
</script>
